* Son 1: Born Feb 1969 in Jodhpur (interviewer's father)  
* Son 2: Born in Jodhpur (Banu/Banoo)  
* Son 3: Born 1974 in Kota (Bhayu/Bhanu)

**Grandchildren:**

* Multiple grandchildren including the interviewer

## **Achievements & Legacy**

‚ú® **Education:** MA Economics, B.Ed ‚ú® **Skills:** Teaching, Music, Cooking, Tailoring, Gardening, Astrology ‚ú® **Values:** Strong moral character, spirituality, self-reliance ‚ú® **Longevity:** 81 years old with good health (excellent teeth and eyes) ‚ú® **Dedication:** 42 years in same house in Jaipur ‚ú® **Service:** Devoted entire life to family education and development

 ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•â‡§™‡•Ä ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ú ‡§≠‡§∞‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Ç ‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡•ã   
 ‡§†‡•Ä‡§ï ‡§π‡•à   
 ‡§Ø‡•á ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•ã   
 ‡§Ø‡•á ‡§ï‡•â‡§™‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à ‡§ú‡§Ø ‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•É‡§∑‡•ç‡§£‡§æ   
 ‡§π‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§π‡§æ‡§Ç   
 ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§á‡§∏‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç‡§®‡•á ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§æ ‡§≠‡§∞ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ø‡§π‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§§‡§ï

 ‡§§‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ñ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•à 10 ‡§§‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ñ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ï‡§Ç‡§™‡•ç‡§≤‡•Ä‡§ü ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ö‡•Å‡§ï‡§æ

## **Family Heritage**

### **Parents**

* **Father:** Sriram Bhargava (born 1901\)  
  * Worked as Mailguard in the Railway  
* **Mother:** Narayani Bhargava (from Uttar Pradesh)

### **Grandparents**

* **Paternal Grandmother:** Born in Kasauli, Himachal Pradesh  
* **Paternal Grandfather:** Hardayal Singh Bhargava, born in Rewari, Haryana

### **Siblings (7th of 8 children)**

1. Vijayshankar Bhargava (+16 years older)  
2. Sharada Bhargava (+14 years older)  
3. Shivshankar Bhargava  
4. Gorishankar Bhargava  
5. Shushila Bhargava (+5 years older)  
6. Harishankar Bhargava (+2.5 years older)  
7. **Kailash Bhargava (Dadi)**  
8. Kanti Bhargava (-2 years younger)

### **Own Family**

* **Husband:** Married in 1967  
* **Children:**  
  * Tinu Bhargava (born February 1969, Jodhpur)  
  * Binu Bhargava (born 1971, Jodhpur)  
  * Bhaiyu Bhargava (born 1973, Kota)

## **Major Life Timeline**

| Year | Age | Event |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| **1941** | 0 | Born on November 8 in Dariba Kalan, Chandni Chowk, Delhi |
| **1947** | 6 | Witnessed India-Pakistan partition and Hindu-Muslim conflicts |
| **1955** | 16 | Started higher secondary education in Delhi |
| **1961-1964** | 20-23 | BA Honours in Economics at Ramjas College, Delhi |
| **1963** | 22 | NCC rifle training during college |
| **1967** | 26 | Married; moved to Jodhpur |
| **1968** | 27 | Earned MA in Economics from Agra University |
| **1968** | 27 | First teaching position (July-December) at Nalvana School, Jodhpur |
| **1969** | 28 | Birth of first child, Tinu |
| **1970-1971** | 29-30 | Completed BEd in Jodhpur |
| **1971** | 30 | Birth of second child, Binu |
| **1973** | 32 | Birth of third child, Bhaiyu; moved to Kota |
| **1975** | 34 | Brief stay in Ajmer (6 months) |
| **1976-1981** | 35-40 | Taught at St. Paul's Senior Secondary School, Udaipur (5 years) |
| **1978** | 37 | Food Preservation course in Udaipur |
| **1981** | 40 | Cookery & Bakery course in Jaipur; moved to Jaipur permanently |
| **1987** | 46 | Cutting/knitting and clothing course (6 months) |
| **2001** | 60 | Jyotish (Astrology) course |
| **2013** | 72 | First visit to America |
| **2026** | 84 | Passed away on February 6 |

---

## **Education Journey**

### **Primary Education (1947-1955)**

**Gangapur Station School, Gangapur, Rajasthan**

* Grades 1-8  
* Walked 2-3 kilometers to school daily  
* **Favorite Subjects:** All subjects (English, Hindi, Mathematics)

### **Secondary Education (1955-1958)**

**Government Girls Higher Secondary School**

* Location: Bela Road, Delhi (near Gandhi Samadhi and Ghata Masjid)  
* Grades 9-11  
* Traveled by bus (10 rupees/month), later walked (\~30 minutes)  
* Also attended: Raj Ghat Girls School and Government Higher Secondary Daryaganj School

### **Higher Education (1961-1964)**

**Ramjas College, Morris Nagar, Delhi**

* **Degree:** BA Honours in Economics  
* **Marks:** 60%  
* **Subjects:**  
  * Economics (Major)  
  * Hindi (Compulsory)  
  * English (Compulsory)  
  * Political Science (Optional)  
* **Special Activities:**  
  * NCC (National Cadet Corps) \- all 3 years  
  * Rifle training in 3rd year  
  * Music classes in 2nd year  
  * First Aid course  
  * Kitchen garden activities (won prize)  
* **Class Composition:** 4 girls out of 22 total students  
* **College Experience:** Studied development of USA, Russia, Japan; learned about India as a developing nation

### **Post-Graduate Education (1965-1968)**

**MA in Economics**

* Took exams at Meerut University in Ghaziabad  
* Received degree from Agra University in 1968

### **Professional Training (1970-1971)**

**BEd \- Jodhpur**

* Teaching subjects: Statistics, Optional teaching methods

---

## **Professional Career**

### **Teaching Timeline**

#### **Early Career (1968)**

**Nalvana School, Jodhpur** (July-December 1968\)

* Taught 8th grade: Geometry, Algebra, Arithmetic  
* Taught without textbooks  
* Salary: 105 rupees (before BEd)  
* Stayed with older sister during this time

#### **Post-BEd Career (1970-1981)**

* Salary increased to 250 rupees after completing BEd  
* Private tuitions in mathematics (Algebra, Geometry, Arithmetic)  
* Used abacus and paper/pencil methods

#### **Major Teaching Position (1976-1981)**

**St. Paul's Senior Secondary School, Udaipur**

* 5 years of service  
* Located at Bhatji ki Badi  
* Taught about international development and India's growth as a developing nation  
* Focus on natural resource management and scrutiny

### **Additional Courses & Certifications**

| Year | Course | Location | Duration |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| 1978 | Food Preservation (toffee, candy making) | Udaipur | Short course |
| 1981 | Government of India Cookery & Bakery (pizza, cake) | Jaipur | 1 month |
| 1987 | Cutting/Knitting & Clothing (frocks, blouses, nightsuits, kids' clothes) | ‚Äî | 6 months |
| 2001 | Jyotish (Astrology) | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |

---

## **Family Life Timeline**

### **Marriage & Early Family Years (1967-1973)**

**Jodhpur Era (1967-1973)**

* Married in 1967  
* Address: 3rd A Road, Sardarpura, Jodhpur, Rajasthan  
* February 1969: Tinu born  
* 1971: Binu born  
* Balanced teaching career with raising young children

**Kota Years (1973-1975)**

* 2 years in Gumanpura, Kota, Rajasthan  
* 1973: Bhaiyu born  
* Children attended St. Paul's Sr Secondary School (Kindergarten)

**Ajmer (1975)**

* Brief 6-month stay  
* Lived in a big house  
* Tinu attended school here  
* Husband progressed in career: Supervisor ‚Üí Special Assistant ‚Üí Officer ‚Üí Manager

**Udaipur (1976-1981)**

* 5 years  
* Dadi taught at St. Paul's Senior Secondary School  
* Managed household duties: puja, groceries, childcare

### **Permanent Settlement in Jaipur (1981-2026)**

**Initial Move (End of 1981\)**

* Briefly stayed at RTDC Hotel Gangaur  
* Then Lumba ka makan (faced challenges with landlord)  
* Finally settled in permanent home

**Current Home**

* 42 years in the same house (1981-2023)  
* Created a stable family base

---

## **Places Called Home**

### **1\. Delhi \- Birth & Early Childhood (1941-1955)**

**Dariba Kalan, Chandni Chowk**

* Birthplace: Cycle Market (also known as Splendid Road)  
* Address: 152 Katara Mashru Dariva Kala, Old Delhi  
* Family purchased house 86 years prior  
* Lived there from 1956-1967

**Living Conditions:**

* No running water or electricity  
* Entire family slept in one big room  
* Daily chore: Carrying 32 liters of water on a wooden stick

**Family Arrangement:**

* 4 older siblings stayed with their grandmother in Delhi  
* 4 younger siblings (including Dadi) stayed with father in Gangapur

### **2\. Gangapur, Rajasthan \- Childhood (1940s-1950s)**

**Family Home:**

* Small bungalow  
* Large house with 3 rooms and a big veranda  
* Father worked as Railway Mailguard

### **3\. Jodhpur, Rajasthan (1967-1973)**

* First married home  
* 3rd A Road, Sardarpura  
* Where first two children were born

### **4\. Kota, Rajasthan (1973-1975)**

* Gumanpura area  
* 2 years raising young family

### **5\. Ajmer, Rajasthan (1975)**

* 6 months only  
* Big house  
* Transitional period

### **6\. Udaipur, Rajasthan (1976-1981)**

* 5 years  
* Professional teaching career flourished  
* St. Paul's Senior Secondary School, Bhatji ki Badi

### **7\. Jaipur, Rajasthan (1981-2026)**

* **Permanent home for 42 years**  
* Final resting place

### **8\. United States**

* Visited 5 times  
* First visit in 2013 (age 72\)  
* Last visit in 2024

---

## **Childhood Memories**

### **Historical Context**

* Witnessed the India-Pakistan partition (1947)  
* Saw conflicts between Muslims and Hindus, Pakistanis and Indians  
* Fights originated in her neighborhood  
* No telephones existed during her childhood

### **Daily Life**

**Water Collection:**

* No running water in the house  
* Carried 32 liters of water daily on a wooden stick  
* This was Dadi's primary household responsibility

**School Journey:**

* Walked 2-3 kilometers to school each day  
* No transportation available

**Currency System (Historical):**

* 64 chousat paise \= 1 rupee  
* 16 ek anni \= 1 rupee  
* 8 do anni \= 1 rupee  
* 4 chawanni \= 1 rupee  
* 2 atthanni \= 1 rupee  
* 2 ana \= 1 rupee

### **Family Challenges**

* Father retired during her college years  
* Struggled to get fees from father for education  
* Faced discrimination against girls' education  
* Despite challenges, persevered through BA and MA

---

## **Interests & Hobbies**

### **Sports & Games**

**School Sports:**

* Throwball (9th-11th grade) \- similar to baseball  
* Hit the ball with bat, run to bases

**Traditional Games:**

* Kabaddi  
* Gulli Danda  
* Cards (learned from her grandmother who loved cards):  
  * Court Piece  
  * Chakdi  
  * Rummy

### **Personal Preferences**

**Favorite Color:** Sky Blue

**Favorite Animal:** Parrot (Pakshi)

* Slightly scared of feeding rotis to cows

**Favorite Food:** Roti Sabji

**Favorite Academic Subject:** All subjects\! (English, Hindi, Mathematics)

### **Skills & Activities**

**Mathematics:**

* Expert in Abacus  
* Algebra, Geometry, Arithmetic  
* Paper and pencil calculations

**Music:**

* Took music classes in college (2nd year)

**Professor Julka:**

* Mentioned as favorite or influential professor

---

## **Daily Routine in Later Years**

### **Morning**

* Clean everything in the house  
* Take shower using bucket  
* Fold blankets and organize

### **Evening (7 PM)**

* Daily Aarti  
* Visit Lakshman, Hanuman, and Ganesh temples  
* Receive prasad  
* Return home

### **Dinner**

* Family meal time

### **Philosophy**

* Wanted to enjoy cleaning, cooking, and taking care of the house  
* Took pride in maintaining hygiene  
* Considered it similar to "Sanyas Ashram" \- finding joy in service

---

## **Life Lessons & Philosophy**

### **Core Values Dadi Lived By**

**Generosity:**

"When having food, give to others"

**Honesty:**

"Don't steal from anyone for anything"

**Truthfulness:**

"Don't lie"

### **Historical Knowledge**

**Food & Health:**

* Sugarcane was used for keeping teeth healthy  
* Traditional wisdom and practices

---

---

## **Legacy**

Kalpana Bhargava lived through:

* India's partition and independence  
* India's development as a nation  
* Massive technological and social changes (from no electricity to the digital age)  
* Educational advancement for women (being one of 4 girls in a class of 22\)

She was:

* An educated woman in an era when women's education was rare  
* A dedicated teacher who inspired students  
* A loving mother who raised three children while pursuing her career  
* A grandmother who instilled values of hard work and integrity  
* A woman who found joy in simple daily rituals and service

**Her journey from carrying water on wooden sticks in Old Delhi to visiting America five times represents not just her personal growth, but the transformation of India itself.**

---

*In loving memory*  
 *November 8, 1941 \- February 6, 2026*
